  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_681ef804-ba6f-4764-950a-3ddaa9f8265d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer4553839963832708428">Magnus Chase, a once-homeless teen, is a resident of the Hotel Valhalla and one of Odin's chosen warriors. As the son of Frey, the god of summer, fertility, and health, Magnus isn't naturally inclined to fighting.   <span id="freeText4553839963832708428" style="display:none">Magnus Chase, a once-homeless teen, is a resident of the Hotel Valhalla and one of Odin's chosen warriors. As the son of Frey, the god of summer, fertility, and health, Magnus isn't naturally inclined to fighting. But he has strong and steadfast friends, including Hearthstone the elf, Blitzen the dwarf, and Samirah the Valkyrie, and together they have achieved brave deeds, such as defeating Fenris Wolf and battling giants for Thor's hammer, Mjolnir. Now Magnus faces his most dangerous trial yet. His cousin, Annabeth, recruits her boyfriend, Percy Jackson, to give Magnus some pointers, but will his training be enough?<br /><br />Loki is free from his chains. He's readying <i>Naglfar</i>, the Ship of the Dead, complete with a host of giants and zombies, to sail against the Asgardian gods and begin the final battle of Ragnarok. It's up to Magnus and his friends to stop him, but to do so they will have to sail across the oceans of Midgard, Jotunheim, and Niflheim in a desperate race to reach <i>Naglfar</i> before it's ready to sail. Along the way, they will face angry sea gods, hostile giants, and an evil fire-breathing dragon. But Magnus's biggest challenge will be facing his own inner demons. Does he have what it takes to outwit the wily trickster god?</span>
  <a data-text-id="4553839963832708428" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    Percy and Annabeth appear at the beginning of the book. He gives Magnus some lessons on how to fall into the water from the rigging of the USS Constitution (which gets Magnus killed one time; Alex rushes him back to Valhalla so he can die in there and not die for good). Percy mentions that his mom gave birth to a baby girl named Estelle. Also, Sumarbrander aka Jack tries to come on to Riptide, who he says is female. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The author announced that Magnus Chase book 3 is titled Ship of the Dead, and is set for release on October 3, 2017 (exactly one year away)! He said t<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The author announced that Magnus Chase book 3 is titled Ship of the Dead, and is set for release on October 3, 2017 (exactly one year away)! He said that the current plan is for this to be the final book in the series.<br /><br />He also reminded us that Trials of Apollo book 2 is titled The Dark Prophecy, and it’ll be out in May 2017. Jason Grace will be appearing again, Riordan said, adding that they may one day get a story of their own.<br /><br />There will be five books in the Trials of Apollo series.<br /><br />from: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.hypable.com/magnus-chase-book-3-title/">http://www.hypable.com/magnus-chase-b...</a><a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_2621677050" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2621677050" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2621677050?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141342597" href="/book/show/35711311-magnus-chase-and-the-ship-of-the-dead">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2621677050" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13226161791780305141"><i>"I figured something out. You can't hold on to hate forever. It won't do a thing to the person you hate, but it'll poison you, sure enough."</i> <br/><br/>I love this quote! Who would have thought T.J. could be so wise?! And this is just the beginning! For once we actually get to know a little bit of his background story and I was a happy camper to finally find out more about him. About T.J., Halfblood and about Mallory, that is. <br/>In this third and last book they all got a moment to shine and I’m still intrigu</span>
  <span id="freeText13226161791780305141" style="display:none"><i>"I figured something out. You can't hold on to hate forever. It won't do a thing to the person you hate, but it'll poison you, sure enough."</i> <br /><br />I love this quote! Who would have thought T.J. could be so wise?! And this is just the beginning! For once we actually get to know a little bit of his background story and I was a happy camper to finally find out more about him. About T.J., Halfblood and about Mallory, that is. <br />In this third and last book they all got a moment to shine and I’m still intrigued by some of the revelations that were dropped so nonchalantly, especially about Mallory!! *lol*<br /><br />Well anyway there was a short cameo of Percy and Annabeth too and even though I still haven’t read all the "Percy Jackson" books I enjoyed it immensely. XD I didn’t feel spoiled so that definitely shouldn’t keep you from reading the book. Besides their interactions were really nice and I would have loved to see more of them!! =) <br /><br /><i>"Huh." Annabeth shook her head. "All these years sneaking around, and we could've just been ourselves?"<br />"You should always do that." Alex strolled alongside, back in human form, though he still had a few flamingo feathers stuck in his hair. "And you have to flaunt the weird, my friends."</i><br /><br />And did I already tell you how much I love Alex Fierro?! Yes? Well, I’m going to tell you about her/him anyway! *lol* I’m still besotted with Alex Fierro and I doubt that this is going to change anytime soon. As it seems I’m not the only one who loves her/him though. ;-P Alone the way Magnus thinks about Alex is reason enough to expect an awesome ship to sail. But, hold your horses! Before you see them running off into the sunset together Alex needs to decide if she/he really wants to be with Magnus first. Haha! Yeah, Alex is a hard nut to crack. *lol* Poor Magnus! &gt;_&lt;<br /><br /><i>”Also, I kept thinking about Alex Fierro. You know, maybe just a little. Alex was a force of nature, like the snow thunder. She struck when she felt like it, depending on temperature differentials and storm patterns I couldn’t possibly predict. She shook my foundations in a way that was powerful but also weirdly soft and constrained, veiled in blizzard. I couldn’t assign any motives to her. She just did what she wanted. At least, that’s how it felt to me.”</i><br /><br />Still, despite all his confusion he never falters to do what’s right and necessary. Mainly, to stop Ragnarok and to get Loki back in his chains. Something that isn’t all too easy if there are so many other problems along their way. Magnus wouldn’t be the son of Frey if he wouldn’t be able to deal with all of them though. *lol* I can’t even put into words how precious he is and I love my clumsy summer boy so much that it hurts! XD Seriously he is so kind-hearted I can’t even! &lt;333<br /><br /><i>”I had an overwhelming desire to write a letter for Hearth and Blitz: Dear Cosmic Forces, Please excuse my friends from their deadly fate. They are not feeling well today. At the very least, I wanted to outfit them with safety helmets, life jackets and reflective decals before sending them off.”</i><br /><br />I love how much he cares about his friends and even though he’s probably one of the most clumsy heroes I ever met (Well, I think Simon Snow is still worse. *lol*) he always manages to succeed somehow. XD Plus his love for chocolate! Haha! You just gotta adore him for loving his chocolate so much! But that moment where all his glorious clumsiness got a chance to shine?! <b>EPIC!</b> Just epic! *lol* Gosh I laughed so hard! Poor Magnus though! Haha! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[To all of you who already read the book: I’m talking about Magnus accidentally eating the grease from Alderman’s heart! Which was so EWWW, but also so damn funny I couldn’t help but laugh out loud! XD Seriously, how can you even be so damn clumsy?! *lol* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><i>”The most gruesome thing we discovered was in Uncle Randolph’s refrigerator, where expired yogurt, sour milk and mouldy carrots were evolving into a pre-industrial society. Randolph hadn’t even left me any chocolate in the pantry, the old villain.”</i><br /><br />I think Magnus might have killed me a few times over the course of this book and if I’m entirely honest Alex might have killed me even more often than him. &lt;333 Alex Fierro… *sighs dreamily*<br /><br /><i>”I wasn’t going to die without doing that,” she said.</i><br /><br /><b>OH. MY. GODS!!!</b> That scene was awesome! XD And can we once again appreciate what a precious bean Magnus Chase truly is!? He takes every situation in stride and is always there for his friends. He would rather sacrifice himself instead of causing other people harm, he emits summery warmth and he has absolutely no prejudices!!! &lt;333<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>”I’ll be honest. A small part of my brain thought, Alex is male right now. I have just been kissed by a dude. How do I feel about that?<br />The rest of my brain answered: I have just been kissed by Alex Fierro. I am absolutely great with that.”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I wanted to kiss him for that realisation alone! &lt;3 I’m so sad this series is over now and I really would have wished for more! I could have easily read 10 more books about Magnus and his friends and it still wouldn’t be enough. *lol* Please Uncle Rick, could you at least grace us with a cameo in other series? That would be awesome! =)<br /><br />And I don’t think I actually have to say this after my review but I’ll say it anyway:<br />I loved Uncle Rick’s Magnus Chase series and I’ll forever crave for more! &lt;333</span>
  <a data-text-id="13226161791780305141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

And when my mead cask is angry, people DIE!....</i><br /><br />those awkward moments...<br /><br />✦ <i>THAT AWKWARD moment when you lock eyes with two friends <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[hanging in cages in a giant’s kitchen. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And one of them recognizes you and begins to shout your name, but you do not want your name shouted.<br />Blitzen staggered to his feet....and yelled, “MAG—”<br />“—NIFICENT!” I bellowed over him. “What beautiful specimens!</i><br /><br />✦ <i>That awkward moment when you jump out a window because your friend jumped out a window, then you remember that your other friend can fly.</i><br /><br />with his magical talking hilarious sensitive sword!<br /><br />Really enjoyed this book! good times full of laughter. <div id="review_1985651884" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1985651884" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1985651884?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1985651884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4260877905592475866"><b>
  <blockquote>“Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1514030329i/24744595._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If I were ten years younger, this book would blow my mind for sure. In The Ship of the Dead, Magnus, Sam, Alex and his fellas must stop Ragnarok before Loki starts sailing the ship. The beginning sounded promising and I could feel there're a lot of mind-blowing packages that were to come, but I felt a bit let down after halfway through this book. It was not what I expected, tbh.<br/><br/>Quests after</span>
  <span id="freeText4260877905592475866" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1514030329i/24744595._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I were ten years younger, this book would blow my mind for sure. In The Ship of the Dead, Magnus, Sam, Alex and his fellas must stop Ragnarok before Loki starts sailing the ship. The beginning sounded promising and I could feel there're a lot of mind-blowing packages that were to come, but I felt a bit let down after halfway through this book. It was not what I expected, tbh.<br><br>Quests after quests. Prophecies after prophecies. Isn't there anything new and fresh to put in? I wonder that after all this time the story goes on, it hasn't developed much. Yet many characters seem to grow up and learn some valuable life lessons, but the way Mr.Riordan manages to tell his story is just dull and boring. Anyway, some part of me still enjoyed it quite enough because I wanted to know the ending and how the gang pulls it off.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You’re a strange person.” <br>“I prefer the term fabulously weird.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494861180ra/22759437.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although the ending is legit anti-climatic. Flyting? Seriously? In addition, toward the last 20%, the story goes so fast I could feel it without any consideration. What I liked in this book? Yeah, I kinda liked Alex even though he/she didn't captivate me that much in the second book but in this one, he incredibly stands out.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“The world will end. The big picture cannot be changed. But in the meantime, as Loki once said, we can choose to alter the details. That’s how we take control of our destiny.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514030470ra/24744609.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ps. If there were any chance that this series would continue, please give me more Thor. I can't get enough of him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4260877905592475866" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141342597" href="/book/show/35711311-magnus-chase-and-the-ship-of-the-dead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=fantasy-scifi">fantasy-scifi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=favourites-2017">favourites-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=queer-books">queer-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=poc">poc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33510193-romie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2133760841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6430593551832770795">Am I okay? Or am I dying because of the feels? Am I reborn in Valhalla?<br/>Those are all great questions.<br/><br/>I didn’t read this book, I inhaled it. Seriously. This book was read in less than a day, that’s simply how good it was. I couldn’t put it down, I NEEDED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENED NEXT.<br/><br/>I loved every single character in this book, and I think what I liked the most was knowing all the stories behind Mallory, T.J. and Gunderson, it was just so meaningful. Those three aren’t really present until this book</span>
  <span id="freeText6430593551832770795" style="display:none">Am I okay? Or am I dying because of the feels? Am I reborn in Valhalla?<br />Those are all great questions.<br /><br />I didn’t read this book, I inhaled it. Seriously. This book was read in less than a day, that’s simply how good it was. I couldn’t put it down, I NEEDED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENED NEXT.<br /><br />I loved every single character in this book, and I think what I liked the most was knowing all the stories behind Mallory, T.J. and Gunderson, it was just so meaningful. Those three aren’t really present until this book, but you learn to love them in just the little time you get to have them.<br /><br />I’m so happy this book took place during Ramadan because it is so important to have representation, it matters. Seeing Samirah fasting, doing her prayers, breaking her fast with dates, focusing on her emotions, it was simply amazing.<br /><br />My small son Maggie, my Mango, my Magnus, I’m so proud of him, this little shit nearly made me cry several times but I love him and of course he’s forgiven. I think it’s the book you get to really see who Magnus actually is : a healer. That’s truly the essence of his being. Magnus is best at healing people, making them feel whole again, important and loved. But being a healer sometimes means you forget about yourself, how amazing and valuable you are . . . you forgot about the greatness there is within you, that’s also Magnus. Magnus who fell in love with the most amazing person ever, I’ve named Alex Fierro.<br /><br />Alex Fierro is a force of nature, that’s truly the best way you can describe her. She’s little but fierce, ready to cut your head off — yeah that’s not a joke, she’ll do it. She’s probably one of the most interesting characters I’ve ever read about, the complexity behind her character is phenomenal. She’s transgender, gender-fluid, our favourite latinx queen, and ready to kick your butt if you dare calling her by the wrong pronouns — especially when she takes the time to tell you which one to use, you punk.<br /><br />Uncle Rick is truly a good ally. That is something you cannot take away from him. He’s respectful of all the different cultures there are out there, and seriously I could cry just because of that. We do not deserve Rick Riordan. We do not. Rick Riordan decided to write diverse characters because that’s the way the world is, and he doesn’t ask to be praised for that. He’s just doing his job has an extremely talented author.<br /><br />Thank you Uncle Rick, you’re so loved.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6430593551832770795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2141944991" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2141944991" />
    <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl"><img alt="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603085284p2/8734459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2141944991?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36126988-magnus-chase-and-the-ship-of-the-dead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=scandinavia">scandinavia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2141944991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2585389375285431254"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507822073i/24152468._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>3.5 stars. Final review, first posted on <a href='http://www.fantasyliterature.com/reviews/the-ship-of-the-dead/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fantasy Literature</a>:<br/><br/>When <i>
  <a href='https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naglfar' rel='nofollow noopener'>Naglfar</a>
</i> ― a ship made out of the fingernails and toenails of the dead, eek! ― sets sail, carrying hordes of giants and zombies warriors to fight the gods of Asgard, Ragnarok and a world-ending battle aren’t far behind. Ragnarok can’t be entirely avoided, unfortunately (it’s an inevitable prophecy), but perhaps it can be delayed for a while longer?<br/><br/>As the third and final book in Rick Riordan‘s MAGNUS CHASE AND THE GODS OF ASGARD</span>
  <span id="freeText2585389375285431254" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507822073i/24152468._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>3.5 stars. Final review, first posted on <a href="http://www.fantasyliterature.com/reviews/the-ship-of-the-dead/" rel="nofollow noopener">Fantasy Literature</a>:<br><br>When <i>
  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naglfar" rel="nofollow noopener">Naglfar</a>
</i> ― a ship made out of the fingernails and toenails of the dead, eek! ― sets sail, carrying hordes of giants and zombies warriors to fight the gods of Asgard, Ragnarok and a world-ending battle aren’t far behind. Ragnarok can’t be entirely avoided, unfortunately (it’s an inevitable prophecy), but perhaps it can be delayed for a while longer?<br><br>As the third and final book in Rick Riordan‘s MAGNUS CHASE AND THE GODS OF ASGARD series begins, Loki has escaped from his imprisonment by the gods and is getting the dreaded ship <i>Naglfar</i> ready to sail against the gods, triggering Ragnarok. Right now the ship is docked between Niflheim (the world of ice and fog) and Jotunheim (the home of the giants), prepared to set sail as soon as Midsummer causes the ice on the sea to melt enough. Loki <i>loves</i> global warming, by the way.<br><br>Clearly Magnus Chase and his friends need to stop him somehow! But first Magnus needs to get some training in battling sea monsters from Percy Jackson, then search his dead uncle’s mansion for a mysterious clue, fight a wolf for its possession, set sail with his einherjar friends on a banana-yellow Viking warship through perilous seas to find and stop Loki, avoid being eaten by the sea giant Aegir and his nine bloodthirsty daughters, take a break to go to Alfheim (home of the elves) to fight a malicious dragon and try to get the magical whetstone of Bolverk from his hoard, then …<br><br>You know what? It’s just another quest for a Riordan demigod hero, and the fun is in going along for the ride. As is typical for Riordan’s YA books, the journey is rather charmingly complex and random, a literary Rube Goldberg chain reaction machine, where one event triggers another, which in turn trips off another, and so on.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507822073i/24152469.jpg" width="400" height="235" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But it’s an enjoyable ride, even if the trip is convoluted and you don’t really remember the specifics of most of these episodic adventures after you’re done reading the book. And sometimes seemingly significant events like, say, developing the ability to understand the speech of animals, are raised and then dropped with little or no explanation or resolution. But Magnus Chase cracks lots of jokes along the way, some of which are actually quite amusing. The chapter titles are always witty; my favorites this time around were “I Inherit a Dead Wolf and Some Underwear,” followed by “But Wait. Act Now, and You Get a <i>Second</i> Wolf Free!”<br><br>The cast of <i>The Ship of the Dead</i> is diversity personified, including once-homeless Magnus; Alex, who frequently shifts back and forth between identifying as male and female; devout Muslim Samirah, who fasts for the month of Ramadan notwithstanding all their troubles and conflicts; former black slave and Civil War soldier Thomas Jefferson (T.J.) Jr.; and more. With all this diversity, there’s a refreshing emphasis on friendship and loyalty. It culminates in the book’s climactic scene, with an unexpected twist befitting this entire series’ theme of unity in diversity.<br><br>Riordan finds creative ways to weave in many actual legends and characters from Norse mythology. I was particularly impressed when I did a little online sleuthing regarding Bolverk, and found that <a href="http://www.norse-mythology.cba.pl/page,48,bolverk.html" rel="nofollow noopener">an ancient legend</a> concerning Bolverk, a whetstone, a battle with slaves and the mead of poetry had been neatly woven into the text of <i>The Ship of the Dead</i>. That Naglfar ship though. *shudders*<br><br><i>The Ship of the Dead</i> wraps up Magnus Chase’s initial story arc, though I’d expect that some of these characters will make an appearance again in later Riordan books. Near the end there’s a teaser involving Percy Jackson and his girlfriend Annabeth, presumably pointing to the next book set in Riordan’s multi-mythological world.<br><br>Content note: Parents of younger readers may want to be aware that the gender-fluid Alex, introduced in the second book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27904311.The_Hammer_of_Thor__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___2_" title="The Hammer of Thor (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #2) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hammer of Thor</a>, becomes romantically involved with another character in this book (trying to avoid too many spoilers here). Kisses only. Regardless of your stance on this hot topic, it's a good one to discuss with your kids.<br><br><i>I received a free copy of this book from the publisher, Disney-Hyperion, for review. Thank you!!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2585389375285431254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1776282789" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1776282789" />
    <a title="ambsreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads"><img alt="ambsreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508924675p2/30813900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1776282789?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1776282789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2746985212373077824"><a href='http://ambsreads.wordpress.com/2017/10/07/ship-of-the-dead-by-rick-riordan-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS ARE ALSO ON MY BLOG</a><br/><br/>R A M B L E<br/><br/>First up, it feels so good to be writing a review. I haven’t finished a book in a while (about a week, actually) so writing this makes me so happy. Life just sucks at the moment, makes it difficult to make time for a book when you’re packing all your stuff and trying to find a house. But, hey, what can you do?<br/><br/>Okay, now fully into the ramble;<br/><br/>Some books you truly want to be longer than a trilogy. The story of Magnus Chase is one of them for me. </span>
  <span id="freeText2746985212373077824" style="display:none"><a href="http://ambsreads.wordpress.com/2017/10/07/ship-of-the-dead-by-rick-riordan-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS ARE ALSO ON MY BLOG</a><br /><br />R A M B L E<br /><br />First up, it feels so good to be writing a review. I haven’t finished a book in a while (about a week, actually) so writing this makes me so happy. Life just sucks at the moment, makes it difficult to make time for a book when you’re packing all your stuff and trying to find a house. But, hey, what can you do?<br /><br />Okay, now fully into the ramble;<br /><br />Some books you truly want to be longer than a trilogy. The story of Magnus Chase is one of them for me. I know absolutely nothing about Norse mythology. Greek, Egyptian and Roman mythology I all knew about so reading Riordan’s other series were made easy by previous knowledge. Norse mythology was a big wide world of nothing for me. The only thing I really knew was Chris Hemsworth played Thor (my mum loves Chris Hemsworth). This series took me a while to get into and to learn the particular gods of this world, but once I was into it I was so completely in love with the characters.<br /><br />Riordan manages to weave challenges into a story that don’t become tiresome and add to the characters overall journey. He creates fresh characters in every series and their backstories will have you in tears. We don’t even get to learn everything throughout this book, simply get glimpses of the other characters while Magnus Chase attempts to stop Ragnarok.<br /><br />We have such a diverse cast of characters particularly throughout this series that it is the perfect middle-grade novel. Almost everyone can find themselves in this book or pieces of themselves which I think is perfect for children who are going through particular things that aren’t the ‘norm’. I can’t speak for any of the rep though, but I believe it is well done from what I’ve read (will hunt for own voices reviews).<br /><br />I really think Riordan’s series is important for the amazing plot and the characters throughout. I may be 20 in a couple months but I can’t stop myself from picking up these books and being completely engaged.<br /><br />P L O T<br /><br />The thing about Riordan’s books is that you can’t say much about the plot without spoiling a whole lot. This book details Magnus and our well-known friends going on a journey to defeat Loki. Of course, nothing goes right and there are several side adventures that keep humour up and myself engaged as a reader.<br /><br />This was the perfect book for me to read at the current time. My family is going through some struggles right now and I am getting my wisdom teeth ripped out on Thursday, so I just need to keep myself distracted (but not too distracted, if that makes sense?).<br /><br />Riordan is one of the best writers for the plot, though. I need the plot to keep me engaged and entertained and never over the five years I’ve been reading his books has he let me down. I just love all the additions to the overall story and the even larger addition of humour. These books will get you smiling and giggling.<br /><br />Also, the romance in this book is one of my favourite romances in every book I’ve ever read. It was cute, sweet and completely relatable. It happens so organically and isn’t forced. The trauma between characters is never disregarded either, which I loved.<br /><br />C H A R A C T E R S<br /><br />#M A G N U S C H A S E <br /><br />I love Magnus Chase with all my heart. He is a character that isn’t the ‘chosen one’ or the son of the most well-known and best god of that particular mythology. He’s a bit of a weenie actually. He makes me laugh so hard and constantly keeps me on my toes with his snarky remarks or embarrassing moments.<br /><br />He truly grows in this book. He comes into his own and discovers more about himself and the other around him. I wish we got more of his grief, though. He has lost so much for such a young child and I would honestly be a wreck if it was me. I am blown away.<br /><br />The way he is such a caring individual as well. I mean, he is the son of a god who heals people, so it makes sense. I don’t know what to say, really. I just adore Magnus Chase. He is a sweetheart and I just want to hug him.<br /><br />#O T H E R S<br /><br />I’ve added in this others bit purely because there are so many other characters in this book. We have Alex, Sam, Blitzen, Hearthstone, Mallory, T.J., Gunderson and Jack. They are all incredibly important throughout this particular story. Making their mark and giving us a bit more information on characters that have felt neglected in the past two books.<br /><br />I particularly liked seeing Sam do Ramadam, it was interesting to have that different spiritual connection throughout the book that focuses on a mythology. Alex becomes a full-fledged character for me, as we learnt about his/her background. It was truly heartbreaking. The same goes as we learn about Mallory, T.J and Gunderson, how they all ended up in Valhalla.<br /><br />I’m not sure what to say, apart from the fact I may love the side characters more than I love Magnus Chase. Wild, right?<br /><br />O V E R A L L<br /><br />Overall, a phenomonal conclusion. It has left me desperately and anxiously wanting more. I can’t wait for Magnus to pop up in other books Riordan does. My only complaint would be, not enough Percy Jackson. I was really hoping the Greek and Norse worlds would have come together in this novel, but oh well, what can I do now? Anxiously await for Riordan’s next release and re-read every book he’s written.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2746985212373077824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2142415722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2142415722" />
    <a title="Hannah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41788446-hannah"><img alt="Hannah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475256742p2/41788446.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2142415722?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah" href="/user/show/41788446-hannah">Hannah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32508903-the-ship-of-the-dead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788446-hannah?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788446-hannah?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2142415722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1385061123593856071">The good thing about Rick Riordan's books is that you always know what you get. They are light-hearted, funny, fast-paced, and just lovely to read. Having said that - I think he might be running out of steam here.<br/><br/>I will not even try to give a synopsis because, like all the books in the Percy Jackson universe before this, it's basically: group of demi-gods (or Einherjar) get send on a quest, they go from place A to place B - get attacked/meet a monster/get challenged - escape, go to place C - get</span>
  <span id="freeText1385061123593856071" style="display:none">The good thing about Rick Riordan's books is that you always know what you get. They are light-hearted, funny, fast-paced, and just lovely to read. Having said that - I think he might be running out of steam here.<br /><br />I will not even try to give a synopsis because, like all the books in the Percy Jackson universe before this, it's basically: group of demi-gods (or Einherjar) get send on a quest, they go from place A to place B - get attacked/meet a monster/get challenged - escape, go to place C - get attacked/meet a monster/ get challenged - escape, go to place D - get attacked/ meet a monster/ get challenged - and so on and so forth. The recipe works; the books are all insanely readable and fun but, especially the later ones get a little bit stale. Not enough that I stop reading them, mind, but enough to make me hope that Rick Riordan will actually manage to wrap them up sooner rather than later so that they can end on a high.<br /><br />What I love about these books is how obviously aware of his readers Rick Riordan is - and he tries to write characters that many people can relate to. I find that especially important in Middle Grade books. He seems to have such a lovely, positive world view and his books reflect that. They always emphasize friendship and being there for each other and being a good person. I like that.<br /><br />I think one of the reasons this book did not quite work for me is the fact how very dark the underlying mythology is: don't get me wrong, the Greek pantheon is filled with dark and twisted tales but also with goodness and hope, Norse mythology? Not so much. It is filled with the knowledge that the end of the world - Ragnarok - is inevitable. And this grimness does not quite mesh with the light-hearted voice of the series. <br /><br />But still, I enjoyed reading this book and spending more time in this world that feels familiar, it is comforting to know exactly what to expect and I needed that.<br /><br />First sentence: "'Try it again,' Percy told me. 'This tme with less dying.'"</span>
  <a data-text-id="1385061123593856071" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2148411620" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2148411620" />
    <a title="Jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/202724-jessica"><img alt="Jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601676054p2/202724.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2148411620?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica" href="/user/show/202724-jessica">Jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/202724-jessica?shelf=middle-grade">middle-grade</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/202724-jessica?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/202724-jessica?shelf=new-favorites">new-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/202724-jessica?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2148411620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8718892982254654424">Oh, Magnus! You are the best!<br/><br/>I have been trying to decide what it is about these that I love so much. I have really, REALLY liked the Percy Jackson and the Heroes of Olympus books, but I LOOOVE Magnus. And I realized that it's because Magnus is, well, such a sweetheart. He is a genuinely compassionate and just sweet guy, and I adore him for that. His first thought, in any situation, is how to take care of his friends. He knows he's not a good fighter, and he doesn't like fighting, so he's always</span>
  <span id="freeText8718892982254654424" style="display:none">Oh, Magnus! You are the best!<br /><br />I have been trying to decide what it is about these that I love so much. I have really, REALLY liked the Percy Jackson and the Heroes of Olympus books, but I LOOOVE Magnus. And I realized that it's because Magnus is, well, such a sweetheart. He is a genuinely compassionate and just sweet guy, and I adore him for that. His first thought, in any situation, is how to take care of his friends. He knows he's not a good fighter, and he doesn't like fighting, so he's always looking for other options and ways they can talk things out, and I adore him for it. He's also funny, but without being mean or snarky, and naive without being stupid. He's the perfect man. <br /><br />I also love how Riordan, through Magnus, points out how completely crazy and occasionally gross Norse mythology is. You know me, you know these are my ancestors, you know I read a lot of Norse mythology. But let's face it: a ship made out of the finger and toenails of the unredeemed dead? That's DISGUSTING. And what would that LOOK like?! The fact that Loki once turned into a beautiful lady horse, and later had an eight-legged horse baby?! That's, as the kids say, completely CRAY-CRAY. <br /><br />And I love the cast of characters in this. Samirah El-Abbas and her magical hijab. Alex and her green and pink fashions. Blitzen and Hearthstone, the ultimate surrogate dad/older brothers. I just melted with love for poor Amir, who is doing his normal human best to not freak the frak out and be supportive of all this, and who brought Magnus a cooler of falafel sandwiches for their deadly quest. Amir! You're awesome!<br /><br />So, if you haven't read this series, DO IT. The first book is The Sword of Summer. If you haven't read any Rick Riordan, go ahead and start with The Sword of Summer, too. Just . . . just read these books, guys. They're great! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8718892982254654424" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2187412365" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2187412365" />
    <a title="Camille ☼" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25663885-camille"><img alt="Camille ☼" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530652209p2/25663885.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2187412365?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Camille ☼" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Camille ☼" href="/user/show/25663885-camille">Camille ☼</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2187412365" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16515724102261848179"><i>“You’re a strange person.”</i><br/><br/><i>“I prefer the term fabulously weird.”</i><br/><br/><b>4.5.</b> I have to admit that I started this series already ready to rage about how it wasn’t as good as <i>Percy Jackson</i> because the <i>Percy Jackson</i> series is one that I hold particularly close to my heart. However, if after the first book I was positively surprised but not impressed, the rest of the series just got better and better and I can almost say I find this just as good as the other series. <br/><br/>This series stands out in how <b>diverse</b> and </span>
  <span id="freeText16515724102261848179" style="display:none"><i>“You’re a strange person.”</i><br /><br /><i>“I prefer the term fabulously weird.”</i><br /><br /><b>4.5.</b> I have to admit that I started this series already ready to rage about how it wasn’t as good as <i>Percy Jackson</i> because the <i>Percy Jackson</i> series is one that I hold particularly close to my heart. However, if after the first book I was positively surprised but not impressed, the rest of the series just got better and better and I can almost say I find this just as good as the other series. <br /><br />This series stands out in how <b>diverse</b> and <b>open-minded</b> it is. How many books have you read that figures characters with different religious beliefs (without any of them being judged for it, or only seen through it), characters with disabilities (and I mean <i>important</i> characters), characters that are gender fluid and characters with different sexualities, and more ? A book that does not make those things the most important thing about these characters. Because what is important is how kind, brave, funny, sassy, and heroic they are. THANK YOU. It felt amazing. I love all of those characters and I would do anything to protect them. Alex, Sam and Hearthstone especially. <br /><br />Concerning the story, like any Rick Riordan’s book it was funny, full of action, taught a lot about North mythology and was overall such an easy and light read. I don’t think I have anything bad to say about this really. I’m really sad that this series is finished because I think I could have read a lot more books about these characters. <br />Guys, if you loved Percy Jackson or if you’re looking for diversity and something different, I can only HIGHLY recommend this.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16515724102261848179" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13851618397436968563">✨ 🌟 5 <i> 'fabulously weird' </i> stars 🌟 ✨ <blockquote> <i> <b> Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth. </b> </i> </blockquote> # 1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724396.The_Sword_of_Summer__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___1_' title='The Sword of Summer (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #1) by Rick Riordan' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Sword of Summer</a> - 4.25 🌟<br/># 2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27904311.The_Hammer_of_Thor__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___2_' title='The Hammer of Thor (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #2) by Rick Riordan' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Hammer of Thor</a> - 4 🌟<br/># 3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28006120.The_Ship_of_the_Dead__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___3_' title='The Ship of the Dead (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #3) by Rick Riordan' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Ship of the Dead</a> - 5 🌟<br/><br/>Ragnarok is almost here, and our heroes must find a way to stop it. This was hands down my favourite book of the series! <blockquote> <b> “I figured something out. You can't hold onto hate forever. It won't do a thing to the person you hate, but it'll poison you, sure enough.” </b> </blockquote> T</span>
  <span id="freeText13851618397436968563" style="display:none">✨ 🌟 5 <i> 'fabulously weird' </i> stars 🌟 ✨ <blockquote> <i> <b> Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth. </b> </i> </blockquote> # 1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724396.The_Sword_of_Summer__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___1_" title="The Sword of Summer (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #1) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sword of Summer</a> - 4.25 🌟<br># 2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27904311.The_Hammer_of_Thor__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___2_" title="The Hammer of Thor (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #2) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hammer of Thor</a> - 4 🌟<br># 3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28006120.The_Ship_of_the_Dead__Magnus_Chase_and_the_Gods_of_Asgard___3_" title="The Ship of the Dead (Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard, #3) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Ship of the Dead</a> - 5 🌟<br><br>Ragnarok is almost here, and our heroes must find a way to stop it. This was hands down my favourite book of the series! <blockquote> <b> “I figured something out. You can't hold onto hate forever. It won't do a thing to the person you hate, but it'll poison you, sure enough.” </b> </blockquote> The final part of the trilogy was *everything* I wanted ❤️ <blockquote> <b> “I think the hardest thing we can ever do is see someone for who they really are. Our parents. Our friends. Ourselves.” </b> </blockquote> Magnus is my favourite Rick Riordan character yet. He is funny, brave, sweet, loyal and there is so much goodness in him that I can't put into words. Several times in this book I wanted to reach out and give him a hug.<br><br>I loved how Magnus wasn't really the best fighter, or wasn't the son of a really famous Norse God. Instead <b> his strength lies in healing people, not just their bodies, but their souls too. </b> I would much rather prefer someone who heals and inspires people, than one who is simply good with a sword! <br><br>I absolutely adored how the relationship between Magnus and Alex unfolded, and my guess of Magnus being a pansexual is finally confirmed! <blockquote> <b> I'll be honest. A small part of my brain thought, <i> Alex is male right now. I have just been kissed by a dude. How do I feel about that? </i><br>The rest of my brain answered: <i> I have just been kissed by Alex Fierro. I am absolutely great with that. </i> </b> </blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599620817i/30080457._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gah! Those two deserve all the happiness in the world.<br><br>In this book we finally get the stories of the other side characters including Mallory, Gunderson and TJ. The only one I missed here was Otis the goat! 😂 I'm going to miss this whole squad so much and I really wish there were more books to this series! <br><br>I rarely rate books a solid 5-star, but this one deserves it. Even though it has a happy ending, it is kind of bittersweet. <blockquote> <b> “The world will end. The big picture cannot be changed. But in the meantime, as Loki once said, we can choose to alter the details. That’s how we take control of our destiny.” </b> </blockquote> <br><br><br>__________________________<br><br><u> Pre-reading: </u><br><br>It's finally time to read the last book! ✨<br><br>I had been putting this off because I'm <i> not </i> ready to say goodbye to my babies 🙈💜😢</span>

  <i>“Wow,"<i> said Samirah as we approached the dock. <i>"You're right, Alex.     <a title="sally ✿" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22377683-sally"><img alt="sally ✿" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605050973p2/22377683.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2060036345?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="sally ✿" class="user" itemprop="url" name="sally ✿" href="/user/show/22377683-sally">sally ✿</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22377683-sally?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22377683-sally?shelf=bookshelf">bookshelf</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2060036345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4839813601421383326"><b>After reading | October 11th, 2017:</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I cried. I actually <i>cried</i> and I’m so embarrassed to admit that I cried because it honestly wasn’t even that sad. I’m just such an emotional trainwreck, and I don't know what is wrong with me.<br/><br/>BUT GOSH DARN IT THE FLYTING SCENE? AND THE OTHALA RUNE SCENE?<br/><br/>My heart was just hit with all of the feels and I couldn’t help myself.<br/><br/>This trilogy has been just </span>
  <span id="freeText4839813601421383326" style="display:none"><b>After reading | October 11th, 2017:</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Sometimes you lie to deceive people. Sometimes you lie because you need the lie to become the truth.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I cried. I actually <i>cried</i> and I’m so embarrassed to admit that I cried because it honestly wasn’t even that sad. I’m just such an emotional trainwreck, and I don't know what is wrong with me.<br /><br />BUT GOSH DARN IT THE FLYTING SCENE? AND THE OTHALA RUNE SCENE?<br /><br />My heart was just hit with all of the feels and I couldn’t help myself.<br /><br />This trilogy has been just so heartwarming and sweet and hilarious and I love all of the diversity and the friendships and the love, and I don’t know. I am happy.<br /><br />I am hopeful.<br /><br />I am satisfied.<br /><br />I’m so sad it’s over. I am going to miss the bravery that is Samirah al-Abbas, and the adorableness that is her and Amir. I am going to miss Blitzen and Hearthstone who are the true heroes. I am going to miss Alex Fierro who constantly changes but is always true to who they are. I am going to miss Mallory, TJ and Halfborn who have been through so much, but are so loyal and the best friends anyone could ask for.<br /><br />And most of all, I am going to miss the sunshine and sweetness that is Magnus Chase. I am so proud of these nerds, I will miss them all so much.<br /><br />I really hope it’s not the last we hear from the all the einherjar! <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You can't hold onto hate forever. It won't do a thing to the person you hate, but it'll poison you, sure enough.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />-----<br /><br /><b>Before reading | July 18th, 2017:</b><br /><br /><b>Me after finishing Sword of Summer:</b> okay, I'm actually totally on board with Magnus not having a love interest.<br /><br /><b>Me after finishing Hammer of Thor:</b> ASDFGHJKL SHIP SHIP SHIP<br />GIVE ME MORE ALEX FIERRO<br /><br />My hopes for Ship of the Dead:<br />≫ BEATRICE (Rick has officially dubbed them this, pass it on)<br />≫ Blitzstone to be confirmed (I mean, were you not feeling those vibes in Hammer of Thor? Because it one hundred percent seems like they have feelings for each other)<br />≫ more Loki (I hate him, but I love him)<br />≫ Percy Jackson to be besties with all the einherjar (I hope him and Magnus will become best friends?? They have similar sassy personalities, but I don't know if Percy will be able to get over the fact that Magnus hates the color blue)<br /><br />(by the way, can we just talk about how Magnus Chase shares a name with Magnus Bane who is in love with Alec Lightwood? Malec and Malex? And Rick also dedicated the first book to Cassie which means they're friends and probably messing with us)</span>
  <a data-text-id="4839813601421383326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8974994869008650232">I'm sad to be done with Rick's Norse books. These were wonderful. Rick's writing is so clear and he has such a deep understanding of mythology to be able to play with the gods the way he does. These are some of my favorite books as I love anything having to do with mythology. I also enjoy that Magnus is a healer. It's nice that he heals.<br/><br/>Also, I think Alex is one of the coolest characters in literature. I mean, it's so neat that he/she is allowed to flow back and forth on the gender spectrum. It'</span>
  <span id="freeText8974994869008650232" style="display:none">I'm sad to be done with Rick's Norse books. These were wonderful. Rick's writing is so clear and he has such a deep understanding of mythology to be able to play with the gods the way he does. These are some of my favorite books as I love anything having to do with mythology. I also enjoy that Magnus is a healer. It's nice that he heals.<br /><br />Also, I think Alex is one of the coolest characters in literature. I mean, it's so neat that he/she is allowed to flow back and forth on the gender spectrum. It's also amazing that Magnus is attracted to him/her and it's the person. I love it. Rick also tackles homelessness in this book. It is such a well done book. <br /><br />They have to face off against Loki in a Flyting to prevent Ragnarok. They go through some rough realms to get there. It starts off at a fast pace and keeps that up. The stakes are high and the action is packed. Magnus has a capable team of adventurers. <br /><br />I'm glad this was my final book for 2017. Hello 2018. Happy New Year. </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1791977101" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1791977101" />
    <a title="Taylor" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52489703-taylor"><img alt="Taylor" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542815566p2/52489703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1791977101?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taylor" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taylor" href="/user/show/52489703-taylor">Taylor</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52489703-taylor?shelf=2017-books">2017-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52489703-taylor?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52489703-taylor?shelf=lgbtqia">lgbtqia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52489703-taylor?shelf=mythology-books">mythology-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52489703-taylor?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1791977101" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6969284015971389415"><i>“The world will end. The big picture cannot be changed. But in the meantime, as Loki once said, we can choose to alter the details. That’s how we take control of our destiny.”</i><br/><br/>...<br/><br/><i>The Ship of the Dead</i> is the third and final book in the Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard trilogy. <b>I'm so unbelievably sad to say that</b>. Truly, this series is so special, wonderful, funny, and heartwarming. <b>I CAN'T BELIEVE IT'S OVER. <i>I DON'T WANT IT TO BE OVER.</i></b><br/><br/>*curls into a fetal position and cries*<br/><br/>Ah. The emotional tur</span>
  <span id="freeText6969284015971389415" style="display:none"><i>“The world will end. The big picture cannot be changed. But in the meantime, as Loki once said, we can choose to alter the details. That’s how we take control of our destiny.”</i><br /><br />...<br /><br /><i>The Ship of the Dead</i> is the third and final book in the Magnus Chase and the Gods of Asgard trilogy. <b>I'm so unbelievably sad to say that</b>. Truly, this series is so special, wonderful, funny, and heartwarming. <b>I CAN'T BELIEVE IT'S OVER. <i>I DON'T WANT IT TO BE OVER.</i></b><br /><br />*curls into a fetal position and cries*<br /><br />Ah. The emotional turmoil. But oh, was the pain worth it. <b>Because this book was amazing</b>.<br /><br />At this point, I shouldn't be surprised. I've been reading Rick's books since I was 12. I remember cracking open <i>The Lightning Thief</i> on Christmas night and being whisked away to a world of gods and monsters, heroes and villains, friendships and unbelievably contagious humor. <b>And Rick hasn't lost his step since</b>. He continues to write books that warm my heart and speak to me on a deep, emotional level. <br /><br />He also continues to make me laugh my ass off. I'm a 19 year old college student, dammit. The fact that Riordan can still make me laugh until I cry is astonishing. <br /><br />But what makes <i>The Ship of the Dead</i> so special?<br /><br />For one, the characters in this novel continue to endear me, and I adored their growth. Hearth and Blitzen are my precious, precious babies and <b>I WOULD DO ANYTHING FOR THEIR HAPPINESS</b>. Anything. I care about them so damn much. Their friendship means <i>everything</i> to me.<br /><br />Samirah al Abbas, our beautiful Muslim Valkyrie, is freakin' <b>business</b>. You don't mess with Samirah or her friends without getting her glowing staff shoved up your ass. <b>I love her</b>. Her unshakable faith and morality was so admirable, considering her godly parentage (I'm talking to you, Loki), and the fact that she was fasting for the holy month of Ramadan throughout the entirety of the quest. <b>How could you get any more badass than that?</b> <br /><br />Magnus' hallmates, which include Thomas Jefferson Jr., Mallory Keen, and Halfborn Gunderson, were all wonderful and my love for them has only grown since the previous books. In <i>The Ship of the Dead</i> especially, we get some welcome development with each of them and their backstories. Mallory isn't just a fiery, knife wielding Irish girl. Halfborn isn't just a muscly berserker who could snap you like a toothpick if he wanted to. TJ is more than just a chipper ex-civil war soldier. Each of them were developed and given weight, and I loved their friendships with Magnus and the roles they played in this story.<br /><br />And then there's Alex Fierro. <b>Someone hold me</b>. I love Alex so <b>DAMN MUCH</b>. Alex is a badass, gender-fluid artist with a garrot as a weapon and a really daring sense of fashion. Don't mess with her. And by the gods, don't get in a war of words with them. <b>Because you'll lose</b>. Alex is fierce and loyal and loving and <b>AHHHH</b>. I CAN'T.<br /><br />And who am I forgetting? Oh right. Our one and only Magnus Chase. <br /><br />Oh Magnus, my sweet, precious child. I know I've said this about every character, but I <b>truly love Magnus.</b> Very deeply. He's a standout in this book for sure, and his growth throughout this series makes my heart swell with pride. He may rely on his talking, self-wielding sword Jack to defend himself, and he may not be a fighter or a warrior. But he's a healer. And he's <b>kind, funny, caring, and oh-so-lovable</b>. Magnus would do anything for his friends, and I would do anything for him.<br /><br />Another exceptional aspect of this book were the relationships between our wonderful characters. <b>The friendships</b>. They <i>killed</i> me. All of the characters on our quest have unbelievable chemistry. The dialogue between Magnus and his friends was <i>hilarious</i>. You truly get the sense that these people care about one another, and I adored the fact that the crew in this book was basically a found family. <b>I even teared up a couple of times</b>.<br /><br /><i>"I faced Hearthstone. I put my hand gently on his chest, an elfish gesture of deep affection. <b>You</b>, I signed. <b>Safe. Or me. Angry.</b><br /><br />The corners of his mouth pulled upward, though he still looked distracted and worried. His heartbeat fluttered under my fingertips like a scared dove. <br /><br /><b>You too</b>, he signed."</i><br /><br />*cries*<br /><br />And can we just talk about Alex and Magnus for a second? Because <b>oh my God</b>. They were so. STINKIN'. <b>CUTE</b>. I ship them <b>
  <i>so hard</i>
</b> man. And damn were they great here. Their relationship was never angsty or corny. It wasn't drenched in stupid clichés. It was realistic and so damn cute. *sighs* My babies deserve all the happiness.<br /><br />The plot never let up. I was never bored, never waiting for the story to progress. When there wasn't a kickass action scene or awesome bits of back and forth dialogue among the characters, there were quieter moments that established the themes of this book beautifully. How families don't always have to be connected by blood. How our pasts can haunt us and shape us into who we are. <b>How our loved ones never truly leave us, even in death.</b><br /><br />And the <b>diversity</b>. Holy shit. TJ and Blitzen are black. Alex is gender fluid. Hearth is deaf. Sam is Muslim. Quite a few of our characters, including Magnus, are queer. Thank you for this, Rick. <b>Thank you</b>.<br /><br />The fact that <i>The Ship of the Dead</i> is the conclusion to Magnus and his friends' stories makes me so sad. But I must say, the journey was wonderful. The ending was equal parts heartwarming and bittersweet, and the tension-filled climax went places that I didn't expect. I hope that this isn't the last time I'll be able to see these lovely characters, but if it is, I'm glad to say that this conclusion was a proper send off.<br /><br />I absolutely adored this book. The Magnus Chase series has burrowed itself into my heart, and will stay with me for a long time. <b>Hopefully forever</b>. <br /><br />Now if you'll excuse me, I'm going to go look up Magnus and Alex fanart.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6969284015971389415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1731343610?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*Thea &#39;Wookiee&#39;sMama&#39; Wilson*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*Thea &#39;Wookiee&#39;sMama&#39; Wilson*" href="/user/show/2791987-thea-wookiee-smama-wilson">*Thea &#39;Wookiee&#39;sMama&#39; Wilson*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1731343610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9406041985002307387">Wow.... Rick Riordan strikes again with another outstanding adventure with Magnus Chase!<br/><br/>This book is a genuine gem and stuffed full of humour that I got some really odd looks from my hubby while giggling over it like a mad woman but you can't help but giggle at and fall a little in love with Magnus and his mental escapades.<br/><br/>Now, I haven't read the Percy Jackson books yet, yes I know it's my bad and I will read eventually, so I can't really say how these compare to those original Riordan adventure</span>
  <span id="freeText9406041985002307387" style="display:none">Wow.... Rick Riordan strikes again with another outstanding adventure with Magnus Chase!<br /><br />This book is a genuine gem and stuffed full of humour that I got some really odd looks from my hubby while giggling over it like a mad woman but you can't help but giggle at and fall a little in love with Magnus and his mental escapades.<br /><br />Now, I haven't read the Percy Jackson books yet, yes I know it's my bad and I will read eventually, so I can't really say how these compare to those original Riordan adventures but I can say that these Norse based tales are brilliant, he twists those Norse Myths to fit his story and his crew of diverse and vivid characters. The world building is impeccable with all that wealth of legend behind it and Riordan's knack for pacing is just fabulous.<br /><br />All in all The Ship Of The Dead is a wonderful, funny and exciting inclusion to the Magnus Chase series..... hurry up and write more soon Mr Riordan!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9406041985002307387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UFMk+wR0P5znHB5J00vHeBpdZG1LovllUdN7zeSOrxa3yUsO+kckiKG7/3tbCWQNQmdspWqoCYJDmSBO+RzMRg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3r6ytmax8j2A8k9vy+W4LioQG2CLdyQqFTVCWOe4pgg5JN1DmILpKcZVrl1DpxtbcioTqKp91M0Hfxnb+irFWA==')})
  }
//]]>
